namespace = company

#Manage Trading Company
country_event = {
        id = company.0
	title = "company.0.t"
	desc = "company.0.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Found a new company
                     name = "company.0.a" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 33
		     }
                     country_event = { id = company.10 }
        }
        option = {   #Manage existing company
                     name = "company.0.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
                                             has_country_flag = india_private_company
											 has_country_flag = india_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = indonesia_private_company
											 has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = china_private_company
											 has_country_flag = china_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = japan_korea_private_company
											 has_country_flag = japan_korea_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = persia_private_company
											 has_country_flag = persia_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = south_africa_private_company
											 has_country_flag = south_africa_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = east_africa_private_company
											 has_country_flag = east_africa_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = west_africa_private_company
                                             has_country_flag = west_africa_official_company
                                   } 
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 33
		     }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Hide Trading Company events
                     name = "company.0.c" 
					 trigger = {
					     NOT = { has_country_flag = hide_tc_event }
						 ai = no
					 }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
             set_country_flag = hide_tc_event
        }
		option = {   #Show Trading Company events
                     name = "company.0.d1" 
					 trigger = {
					     has_country_flag = hide_tc_event
						 ai = no
					 }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
             clr_country_flag = hide_tc_event
        }
        option = {   #Exit
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 33
		     }
                     name = "company.exit" 
        }

}

#Found Trading Company
country_event = {
        id = company.10
	title = "company.1.t"
	desc = "company.1.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Found india company
                     name = "company.1.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
                                             has_country_flag = india_official_company
											 has_country_flag = india_private_company
                                   } 
                                   NOT = {
                                             capital_scope = { 
                                             cu_india_company_region = yes
                                             }
                                   } 
                                   any_owned_province = {
                                             cu_india_company_region = yes
                                             has_port = yes
                                   }
                                   treasury = 100
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 10
                              modifier = {
                                         factor = 0
                                         NOT = { treasury = 200 }
                              }
		     }
                     set_country_flag = found_india_company_1
                     country_event = { id = company.11 }
        }
        option = {   #Found indochina company
                     name = "company.1.b" 
                     trigger = {

#Found Trading Company - official or private
country_event = {
        id = company.11
	title = "company.11.t"
	desc = "company.11.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Found official company
                     name = "company.11.a" 
                     custom_tooltip = company.11.at
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
		     }
                     set_country_flag = found_official_company
                     country_event = { id = company.12 }
        }
        option = {   #Found private company
                     name = "company.11.b" 
                     custom_tooltip = company.11.bt
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
		     }
                     set_country_flag = found_private_company
                     country_event = { id = company.12 }
        }
        option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     clr_country_flag = found_india_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indochina_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indonesia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_china_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_japan_korea_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_persia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_east_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_south_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_west_africa_company_1
                     country_event = { id = company.10 }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
        }
        option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     clr_country_flag = found_india_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indochina_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indonesia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_china_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_japan_korea_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_persia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_east_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_south_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_west_africa_company_1
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
        }

}

#Found Trading Company - Initial Funding
country_event = {
        id = company.12
	title = "company.12.t"
	desc = "company.12.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund 100 ducat
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          treasury = 400
                              }
		     }
                     add_treasury = -100
                     set_country_flag = fund_100
                     country_event = { id = company.13 }
        }
        option = {   #Fund 200 ducat
                     name = "company.fund200" 
                     trigger = { 
                              treasury = 200
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          NOT = { treasury = 400 }
                              }
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          treasury = 1000
                              }
		     }
                     add_treasury = -200
                     set_country_flag = fund_200
                     country_event = { id = company.13 }
        }
        option = {   #Fund 500 ducat
                     name = "company.fund500" 
                     trigger = { 
                              treasury = 500
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
                              }
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          treasury = 2000
                              }
		     }
                     add_treasury = -500
                     set_country_flag = fund_500
                     country_event = { id = company.13 }
        }
        option = {   #Fund 1000 ducat
                     name = "company.fund1000" 
                     trigger = { 
                              treasury = 1000
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 50
                              modifier = {
                                          factor = 0
                                          NOT = { treasury = 2000 }
                              }
		     }
                     add_treasury = -1000
                     set_country_flag = fund_1000
                     country_event = { id = company.13 }
        }
        option = {   #Return
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     clr_country_flag = found_official_company
                     clr_country_flag = found_private_company
                     country_event = { id = company.11 }
        }
        option = {   #Exit
                     ai_chance = {
		  	      factor = 0
		     }
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     clr_country_flag = found_india_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indochina_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_indonesia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_china_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_japan_korea_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_persia_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_east_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_south_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_west_africa_company_1
                     clr_country_flag = found_official_company
                     clr_country_flag = found_private_company
        }

}

#Found Trading Company - Complete
country_event = {
        id = company.13
	title = "company.13.t"
	desc = "company.13.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = { 
                     name = "company.13.a" 
            hidden_effect = {
			         change_variable = { which = num_of_tc value = 1 }
                     if = {
                            limit = { has_country_flag = found_india_company_1 }
                            set_country_flag = india_company
							set_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = india_company_size value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_balance value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_expense value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_income value = 0 }
                            if = {
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = found_official_company
                                    }
                                    set_country_flag = india_official_company
                            }
                            if = {
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = found_private_company
                                    }
                                    set_country_flag = india_private_company
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_100 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 100 }
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_200 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 }
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_500 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 500 }
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_1000 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 1000 }
                            }
                     }
                     if = {
                            limit = { has_country_flag = found_indochina_company_1 }
                            set_country_flag = indochina_company
							set_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = indochina_company_size value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash_total_balance value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash_total_expense value = 0 }

                            if = {
                                    limit = {

                            }
                            if = {
                                    limit = {

                                    set_country_flag = indochina_private_company

                            if = {

                            if = {

                     }
                     if = {

                            set_country_flag = indonesia_company
							set_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 0 }

							set_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash_total_balance value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash_total_expense value = 0 }
							set_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash_total_income value = 0 }
                            if = {

                            }
                            if = {
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = found_private_company
                                    }
                                    set_country_flag = indonesia_private_company
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_100 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 100 }
                            }
                            if = { 
                                    limit = { 
                                             has_country_flag = fund_200 
                                    }
                                    set_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 200 }
                            }
                            if = {

###Trading Company Upgrade
province_event = {
    id = company.21
	title = "company.21.t"
	desc = "company.21.d"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
	      NOT = {
					     owner = { has_country_flag = hide_tc_event }
		  }
	      OR = {  #Minimum CD
				NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = trade_company_spread_cd } }
				owner = { 
						had_country_flag = {
						    flag = trade_company_spread_cd
							days = 30
						}
                }					
		  }
		  OR = {
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
					    has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
						has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
		 }
		 OR = {
					         AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = india_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = indochina_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = china_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = persia_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = west_africa_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = south_africa_company_local
							}
							AND = {
							 
							                 owner = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }  #Cost 50
                                             has_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
							}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	              months = 24
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 5
						  OR = {
						         AND = {
								            owner = { has_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand }
										    cu_india_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {
								            owner = { has_country_flag = indochina_company_focus_expand }
											cu_indochina_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {
                                            owner = { has_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_expand }
											cu_indonesia_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {
                                            owner = { has_country_flag = china_company_focus_expand }
											cu_china_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {
                                            owner = { has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_expand }
											cu_japan_korea_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {
                                            owner = { has_country_flag = persia_company_focus_expand }
											cu_persia_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {
                                            owner = { has_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_expand }
											cu_west_africa_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {
								            owner = { has_country_flag = south_africa_company_focus_expand }
											cu_south_africa_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {
								            owner = { has_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_expand }
											cu_east_africa_company_region = yes
								 }
						  }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 0.66
						  OR = {
						         AND = {
								            owner = { has_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade }
										    cu_india_company_region = yes
								 }
								 AND = {

				  modifier = {
				          factor = 10
						  OR = {

								 }

								 }
								 AND = {
								            owner = { has_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_save }
											cu_east_africa_company_region = yes
								 }
						  }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 3
						  NOT = { is_core = owner }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 1.5
						  NOT = { development = 4 }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 1.5
						  NOT = { development = 6 }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 0.8
						  development = 6
						  NOT = { development = 9 }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 0.6
						  development = 9
						  NOT = { development = 12 }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 0.5
						  development = 12
						  NOT = { development = 15 }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 0.4
						  development = 15
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 0.5
						  OR = {
			                           has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier
                                       has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier_2
                                       has_province_modifier = inland_center_of_trade_modifier
									   has_province_modifier = important_natural_harbor
									   has_province_modifier = river_estuary_modifier
		                  }
				  }
				  modifier = {
				          factor = 0.5
						  OR = {
			                           has_building = marketplace
                                       has_building = trade_depot
                                       has_building = stock_exchange
		                  }
				  }
	}
	immediate = {
	            hidden_effect = {
				           owner = { 
						             clr_country_flag = trade_company_spread_cd  #Refresh Timer
						             set_country_flag = trade_company_spread_cd 
						   }
				}
	}
	option = {
	          name = company.21.a
			  
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_flag = india_company_local }
                      custom_tooltip = company.india_cash_50
					  hidden_effect = { owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = -50 }
                                                  change_variable = { which = india_company_size value = 1 }					  } }
					  
			  }
			  if = {

					  hidden_effect = { owner = { change_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = -50 }
                                                  change_variable = { which = indochina_company_size value = 1 }					  } }
			  }

					  hidden_effect = { owner = { change_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = -50 }

					  hidden_effect = { owner = { change_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = -50 }

					  clr_province_flag = china_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = persia_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = west_africa_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = south_africa_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
			  }
			  
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_off_1
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_off_2
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
			  if = {

                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
					  add_province_modifier = {
					           name = trade_company_off_3
							   duration = -1
					  }
			  }
			  
			  if = { 
			          limit = { has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1 }
                      remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
					  clr_province_flag = india_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = indochina_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
					  clr_province_flag = china_company_local

#Trading Company Yearly Calculation(Hidden)
country_event = {
    id = company.30
	title = "company.30.t"
	desc = "company.30.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
    hidden = yes
    trigger = {
	           NOT = { has_country_flag = trade_company_calculation_reveal }
	           OR = {
                                             has_country_flag = india_private_company
											 has_country_flag = india_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = indonesia_private_company
											 has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = china_private_company
											 has_country_flag = china_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = japan_korea_private_company
											 has_country_flag = japan_korea_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = persia_private_company
											 has_country_flag = persia_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = south_africa_private_company
											 has_country_flag = south_africa_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = east_africa_private_company
											 has_country_flag = east_africa_official_company
                                             has_country_flag = west_africa_private_company
                                             has_country_flag = west_africa_official_company
                }
                is_month = 1
                OR = {
				       NOT = { has_country_flag = trade_company_calculation }
				       had_country_flag = {
					                   flag = trade_company_calculation
					                   days = 335 #prevent accumulated delay
					   }
				}				
	}	
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	        days = 1
				
	}
	immediate = {
	    hidden_effect = {
		    clr_country_flag = trade_company_calculation  #Refresh Timer
	        set_country_flag = trade_company_calculation
	        if = {
			        limit = { 
                              OR = {
							         has_country_flag = india_private_company
									 has_country_flag = india_official_company
							  }
					}
					set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_expense value = 0 }
					set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_income value = 0 } 
					set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_total_balance value = 0 } 
                    set_variable = { which = india_company_size value = 0 }					
			        every_owned_province = {
					          limit = {
							            has_province_flag = india_company_local
										OR = {
										        has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
												has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
										}
							  }
							  #First Calculate Maintanance
							  owner = { set_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 }		  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    OR = {
			                             has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier
                                         has_province_modifier = center_of_trade_modifier_2
                                         has_province_modifier = inland_center_of_trade_modifier
									     has_province_modifier = important_natural_harbor
									     has_province_modifier = river_estuary_modifier
		                                } 
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = marketplace
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.3 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = trade_depot
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.6 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    has_building = stock_exchange
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = 0.9 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    NOT = { development = 6 }
									 } 
									 owner = { change_variable = { which = india_company_cash_expense value = -0.3 } }
							  }
							  if = { 
							         limit = { 
									    development = 9
									 }

								}

						      change_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash which = east_africa_company_cash_balance } 
							  #Automatic Funding
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = -200 } }
											  treasury = 300
									}
									add_treasury = -300
									change_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 300 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = -150 } }
											  OR = {
											          check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = -200 }
													  NOT = { treasury = 300 }
											  }
											  treasury = 250
									}
									add_treasury = -250
									change_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 250 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = -100 } }
											  OR = {
											          check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = -150 }
													  NOT = { treasury = 250 }
											  }
											  treasury = 200
									}
									add_treasury = -200
									change_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 200 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = -50 } }
											  OR = {
											          check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = -100 }
													  NOT = { treasury = 200 }
											  }
											  treasury = 150
									}
									add_treasury = -150
									change_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 150 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 0 } }
											  OR = {
											          check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = -50 }
													  NOT = { treasury = 100 }
											  }
											  treasury = 100
									}
									add_treasury = -100
									change_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 100 } 
							  }
							  if = { 
							        limit = {
							                  has_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
											  NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }
											  treasury = 50
									}
									add_treasury = -50
									change_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 50 } 
							  }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
	       name = "company.30.a"
	}
}

#Manage India Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.41
	title = "company.41.t"
	desc = "company.41.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.41.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								             has_country_flag = india_official_company
											 has_country_flag = india_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.411 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.41.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = india_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.412 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.41.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } } 
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.41.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.41.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.41.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = india_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = india_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.41.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.41.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = india_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.419 }
        }
		option = {   #Return

                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }

                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {

		             }
        }

                     }
					 set_country_flag = india_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.41 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }

                     ai_chance = {

		             }

    id = company.422
	title = "company.422.t"
	desc = "company.422.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Draw 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = 50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = indochina_company_cash value = -50 } }

#Manage indonesia Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.43
	title = "company.43.t"
	desc = "company.43.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.43.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								             has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
											 has_country_flag = indonesia_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.431 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.43.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.432 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.43.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.43.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.43.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.43.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.43.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.43.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.43.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.43.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = indonesia_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.43.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.43.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.439 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund indonesia Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.431
	title = "company.431.t"
	desc = "company.431.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = indonesia_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = indonesia_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = indonesia_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = indonesia_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = indonesia_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = indonesia_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.indonesia_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.43 } }

                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 200 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -100
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = china_company_cash value = 100 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.china_cash_100_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.44 } }
        }

					 custom_tooltip = company.china_cash_500_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.44 } }

#Manage japan_korea Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.45
	title = "company.45.t"
	desc = "company.45.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.45.a" 
                     trigger = {
					               OR = {
								           has_country_flag = japan_korea_official_company
										   has_country_flag = japan_korea_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.451 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.45.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = japan_korea_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.452 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.45.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.45.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.45.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.45.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.45.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.45.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.45.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.45.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = japan_korea_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.45.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.45.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = japan_korea_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.459 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund japan_korea Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.451
	title = "company.451.t"
	desc = "company.451.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = japan_korea_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = japan_korea_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = japan_korea_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = japan_korea_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.45 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }

        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = japan_korea_company_cash value = 50 } }

							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 400 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -200
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 200 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.persia_cash_200_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 500
                     name = "company.fund500" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 500
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -500
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 500 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.persia_cash_500_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 1000
                     name = "company.fund1000" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 1000
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 2000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -1000
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 1000 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.persia_cash_1000_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.46 } }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }

#Manage west_africa Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.47
	title = "company.47.t"
	desc = "company.47.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.47.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = { 
								            has_country_flag = west_africa_official_company
											has_country_flag = west_africa_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.471 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.47.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = west_africa_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.472 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.47.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.47.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.47.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.47.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.47.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.47.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.47.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.47.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = west_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.47.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.47.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = west_africa_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.479 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund west_africa Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.471
	title = "company.471.t"
	desc = "company.471.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = west_africa_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = west_africa_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = west_africa_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = west_africa_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = west_africa_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					          
        }

        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = west_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.west_africa_cash_50_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.47 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 100
                     name = "company.fund100" 
                     trigger = {

							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 1000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -500
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 500 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.south_africa_cash_500_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
        }
		option = {   #Fund 1000
                     name = "company.fund1000" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 1000
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { treasury = 2000 }
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -1000
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = south_africa_company_cash value = 1000 } }
					 custom_tooltip = company.south_africa_cash_1000_inc
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.48 } }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Manage east_africa Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.49
	title = "company.49.t"
	desc = "company.49.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

        option = {   #Fund the company
                     name = "company.49.a" 
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = { 
								            has_country_flag = east_africa_official_company
											has_country_flag = east_africa_private_company
								   }
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 50 }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.491 }
        }
		option = {   #Subtract money from the company
                     name = "company.49.b" 
                     trigger = {
                                   has_country_flag = east_africa_official_company
								   check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 50 }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.492 }
        }
		option = {   #Clear the company's focus
                     name = "company.49.c" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.49.ct
                     trigger = {
                                   OR = {
								          has_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_expand
								          has_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_upgrade
										  has_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.49 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on expansion
                     name = "company.49.d1" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.49.d1t
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_expand
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     set_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.49 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on upgradation
                     name = "company.49.e" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.49.et
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_upgrade
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 200 } }
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_expand
		             set_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.49 } }
        }
		option = {   #Focus on saving
                     name = "company.49.f" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.49.ft
                     trigger = {
                                   NOT = {
								          has_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_save
								   }
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 100 } 
							 }
		             }
                     clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_expand
		             clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_upgrade
					 set_country_flag = east_africa_company_focus_save
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.49 } }
        }
		option = {   #Close the company
                     name = "company.49.z" 
					 custom_tooltip = company.49.zt
                     trigger = {
					               has_global_flag = test_version
                                   has_country_flag = east_africa_official_company
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     #country_event = { id = company.499 }
        }
		option = {   #Return
                     name = "company.ret" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 0
		             }
                     country_event = { id = company.4 }
        }
		option = {   #Exit
                     name = "company.exit" 
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
		             }
        }
}

#Fund east_africa Trading Company
country_event = {
    id = company.491
	title = "company.491.t"
	desc = "company.491.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	    option = {   #Start Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   #has_country_flag = east_africa_official_company
								   NOT = { has_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding }
                     }
					 set_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.49 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					 
                     
        }
        option = {   #Stop Automatic funding
                     name = "company.automaticfund_end"
                     custom_tooltip = company.automaticfund_end.t		 
                     trigger = {
								   has_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
                     }
					 clr_country_flag = east_africa_company_automatic_funding
					 hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = company.49 } }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 100
		             }
					          
        }
	
        option = {   #Fund 50
                     name = "company.fund50" 
                     trigger = {
								   treasury = 50
                     }
                     ai_chance = {
		  	                 factor = 10
							 modifier = {
							       factor = 0
								   NOT = { check_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }
								   treasury = 200
							 }
		             }
                     add_treasury = -50
					 hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = east_africa_company_cash value = 50 } }

#India Trading Company go bankrupt
country_event = {
    id = company.51
	title = "company.51.t"
	desc = "company.51.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
	        has_country_flag = india_company
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = india_company_cash value = 0 } }
			NOT = {
			        any_owned_province = {
					          AND = {
							        has_province_flag = india_company_local
							        OR = {  #Additional check in case of conquered provinces
									      has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
									}
							  }
					}
			}
	}

    option = { #Dust to dust.
            name = "company.5.a" 
			add_prestige = -10
            clr_country_flag = india_company
			clr_country_flag = india_official_company
			clr_country_flag = india_private_company
			hidden_effect = {
			        change_variable = { which = num_of_tc value = -1 }
			        every_owned_province = {
					          limit = {
							        has_province_flag = india_company_local
							  }
							  clr_province_flag = india_company_local
					}
			}
    }
}

							        has_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
							  }
							  clr_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
					}
			}
    }
}

#persia Trading Company go bankrupt
country_event = {
    id = company.56
	title = "company.56.t"
	desc = "company.56.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
	        has_country_flag = persia_company
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = persia_company_cash value = 0 } }
			NOT = {
			        any_owned_province = {
					          AND = {
							        has_province_flag = persia_company_local
							        OR = {  #Additional check in case of conquered provinces
									      has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
										  has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
									}
							  }
					}
			}
	}

    option = { #Dust to dust.
            name = "company.5.a" 
			add_prestige = -10
            clr_country_flag = persia_company
			clr_country_flag = persia_official_company
			clr_country_flag = persia_private_company
			hidden_effect = {
			        change_variable = { which = num_of_tc value = -1 }
			        every_owned_province = {
					          limit = {
							        has_province_flag = persia_company_local
							  }
							  clr_province_flag = persia_company_local
					}
			}
    }
}

#Moving capital to the same continent will remove trading company
province_event = {
    id = company.60
	title = "company.60.t"
	desc = "company.60.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = asia
							}
						}
						continent = asia
					}
					AND = {
						owner = {
							capital_scope = {
								continent = africa
							}
						}
						continent = africa
					}
				}
				
				
				AND = {
						OR = {
							has_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
							has_province_flag = india_company_local
	                        has_province_flag = indochina_company_local
	                        has_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
	                        has_province_flag = china_company_local
	                        has_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
	                        has_province_flag = persia_company_local
	                        has_province_flag = west_africa_company_local
	                        has_province_flag = south_africa_company_local
	                        has_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
						}        
						OR = {  #Additional check in case of conquered provinces
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
						}
				}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
			months = 1
	}
	immediate = {
			clr_province_flag = east_africa_company_local
			clr_province_flag = india_company_local
	        clr_province_flag = indochina_company_local
	        clr_province_flag = indonesia_company_local
	        clr_province_flag = china_company_local
	        clr_province_flag = japan_korea_company_local
	        clr_province_flag = persia_company_local
	        clr_province_flag = west_africa_company_local
	        clr_province_flag = south_africa_company_local
	        clr_province_flag = east_africa_company_local 
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
	}

    option = { #Dust to dust.
            name = "company.5.a"
    }
}

#If official trading company and private trading company appear in the same province, remove the private one.
province_event = {
    id = company.71
	title = "company.71.t"
	desc = "company.71.d"
	picture = TRADECOMPANY_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {				
				AND = {
						OR = {
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_1
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_2
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_3
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_off_4
						}        
						OR = {							
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
							has_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
						}
				}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
			months = 1
	}
	immediate = {
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_1
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_2
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_3
			remove_province_modifier = trade_company_pri_4
	}
	
    option = { #Dust to dust.
            name = "company.5.a"
    }
}
